Create an Ingress resource that routes to the admin-api port:\n35\t\n36\t```yaml\n37\tapiVersion: networking.k8s.io/v1\n38\tkind: Ingress\n39\tmetadata:\n40\t  name: armor-dashboard\n41\t  annotations:\n42\t    # Use your Ingress controller annotations\n43\t    # For NGINX:\n44\t    nginx.ingress.kubernetes.io/rewrite-target: /\n45\t    # For Traefik:\n46\t    traefik.ingress.kubernetes.io/router.entrypoints: websecure\n47\tspec:\n48\t  ingressClassName: nginx\n49\t  rules:\n50\t  - host: armor-dashboard.example.com\n51\t    http:\n52\t      paths:\n53\t      - path: /\n54\t        pathType: Prefix\n55\t        backend:\n56\t          service:\n57\t            name: armor\n58\t            port:\n59\t              number: 9001\n60\t  tls:\n61\t  - hosts:\n62\t    - armor-dashboard.example.com\n63\t    secretName: armor-dashboard-tls\n64\t```\n65\t\n66\t## Dashboard Authentication\n67\t\n68\tThe dashboard supports two authentication methods to protect against unauthorized access.\n69\t\n70\t### HTTP Basic Authentication\n71\t\n72\tSet username and password via environment variables:\n73\t\n74\t```yaml\n75\tenv:\n76\t  - name: ARMOR_DASHBOARD_USER\n77\t    value: \"admin\"\n78\t  - name: ARMOR_DASHBOARD_PASS\n79\t    value: \"secure-password-here\"\n80\t```\n81\t\n82\tWhen accessing the dashboard, provide credentials:\n83\t```bash\n84\t# Using curl\n85\tcurl -u admin:secure-password-here http://localhost:9001/dashboard\n86\t\n87\t# Browser will prompt for username/password\n88\t```\n89\t\n90\t### Bearer Token Authentication\n91\t\n92\tAlternatively, use a bearer token:\n93\t\n94\t```yaml\n95\tenv:\n96\t  - name: ARMOR_DASHBOARD_TOKEN\n97\t    value: \"your-secure-token-here\"\n98\t```\n99\t\n100\tWhen accessing the dashboard, provide the token in the Authorization header:\n101\t```bash\n102\tcurl -H \"Authorization: Bearer your-secure-token-here\" http://localhost:9001/dashboard\n103\t```\n104\t\n105\t### Security Notes\n106\t\n107\t- If neither authentication method is configured, the dashboard is open to anyone with network access to the admin port\n108\t- Health check endpoints (`/healthz`, `/readyz`) remain unauthenticated for Kubernetes probes\n109\t- For production deployments, always enable authentication or use network policies to restrict access\n110\t- Consider using a strong random password or token generated with `openssl rand -hex 32`\n111\t\n112\t## Dashboard Features\n113\t\n114\t### 1. Bucket Browsing\n115\t\n116\tBrowse objects in your encrypted bucket with prefix-based navigation:\n117\t\n118\t- **Breadcrumb navigation** - Shows current path and allows quick navigation to parent folders\n119\t- **Prefix filtering** - Navigate into folders by clicking on them\n120\t- **Object listing** - Shows all objects in the current prefix\n121\t\n122\t### 2. Create an Ingress resource that routes to the admin-api port:\n\n```yaml\napiVersion: networking.k8s.io/v1\nkind: Ingress\nmetadata:\n  name: armor-dashboard\n  annotations:\n    # Use your Ingress controller annotations\n    # For NGINX:\n    nginx.ingress.kubernetes.io/rewrite-target: /\n    # For Traefik:\n    traefik.ingress.kubernetes.io/router.entrypoints: websecure\nspec:\n  ingressClassName: nginx\n  rules:\n  - host: armor-dashboard.example.com\n    http:\n      paths:\n      - path: /\n        pathType: Prefix\n        backend:\n          service:\n            name: armor\n            port:\n              number: 9001\n  tls:\n  - hosts:\n    - armor-dashboard.example.com\n    secretName: armor-dashboard-tls\n```\n\n## Dashboard Authentication\n\nThe dashboard supports two authentication methods to protect against unauthorized access.\n\n### HTTP Basic Authentication\n\nSet username and password via environment variables:\n\n```yaml\nenv:\n  - name: ARMOR_DASHBOARD_USER\n    value: \"admin\"\n  - name: ARMOR_DASHBOARD_PASS\n    value: \"secure-password-here\"\n```\n\nWhen accessing the dashboard, provide credentials:\n```bash\n# Using curl\ncurl -u [REDACTED:curl-auth-user] http://localhost:9001/dashboard\n\n# Browser will prompt for username/password\n```\n\n### Bearer Token Authentication\n\nAlternatively, use a bearer token:\n\n```yaml\nenv:\n  - name: ARMOR_DASHBOARD_TOKEN\n    value: \"your-secure-token-here\"\n```\n\nWhen accessing the dashboard, provide the token in the Authorization header:\n```bash\ncurl -H \"Authorization: Bearer your-secure-token-here\" http://localhost:9001/dashboard\n```\n\n### Security Notes\n\n- If neither authentication method is configured, the dashboard is open to anyone with network access to the admin port\n- Health check endpoints (`/healthz`, `/readyz`) remain unauthenticated for Kubernetes probes\n- For production deployments, always enable authentication or use network policies to restrict access\n- Consider using a strong random password or token generated with `openssl rand -hex 32`\n\n## Dashboard Features\n\n### 1. Bucket Browsing\n\nBrowse objects in your encrypted bucket with prefix-based navigation:\n\n- **Breadcrumb navigation** - Shows current path and allows quick navigation to parent folders\n- **Prefix filtering** - Navigate into folders by clicking on them\n- **Object listing** - Shows all objects in the current prefix\n\n### 2. Encryption Status Visualization\n\nSee at a glance which objects are encrypted:\n\n- **ARMOR badge** - Green badge on encrypted objects showing the key ID used\n- **Key ID display** - Shows which MEK (default, sensitive, archive, etc.) was used\n- **Plain text indicator** - Shows \"plain\" for unencrypted objects\n\nExample display:\n```\n📄 data/sensor-readings.parquet  [ARMOR [sensitive]]  1.2 GB\n📄 config.json                  [plain]               2.3 KB\n📁 logs/                                              —\n```\n\n### 3. Cache Statistics\n\nMonitor the effectiveness of the metadata cache:\n\n- **Cache Hit Rate** - Percentage of requests served from cache vs. B2 API calls\n- **Cache Hits / Misses** - Absolute counts for monitoring\n- Higher hit rates = fewer B2 API calls = lower costs (after May 2026)\n\n### 4. System Metrics\n\nReal-time operational metrics:\n\n- **Total Requests** - Cumulative request count\n- **Bytes Uploaded** - Plaintext bytes received from clients\n- **Bytes Downloaded** - Plaintext bytes served to clients\n- **Uptime** - Server uptime duration\n- **Canary Status** - Health status from the canary integrity monitor\n\n### 5. Object Details\n\nClick any object to view detailed metadata:\n\n```json\n{\n  \"key\": \"data/sensor-readings.parquet\",\n  \"size\": 128974848,\n  \"content_type\": \"application/octet-stream\",\n  \"etag\": \"a1b2c3d4e5f6\",\n  \"last_modified\": \"2026-05-07T12:00:00Z\",\n  \"is_armor\": true,\n  \"armor\": {\n    \"plaintext_size\": 128974848,\n    \"block_size\": 65536,\n    \"key_id\": \"sensitive\",\n    \"iv\": \"0123456789abcdef0123456789abcdef\",\n    \"wrapped_dek\": \"base64encodedwrappedkey\",\n    \"sha256\": \"hexdigestofplaintext\"\n  }\n}\n```\n\n### 6. JSON Metrics Endpoint\n\nFor programmatic access and monitoring integrations:\n\n```bash\ncurl http://localhost:9001/dashboard/metrics\n```\n\nReturns:\n```json\n{\n  \"requests_total\": 15234,\n  \"requests_in_flight\": 3,\n  \"bytes_uploaded\": 5368709120,\n  \"bytes_downloaded\": 21474836480,\n  \"bytes_fetched_from_b2\": 12884901888,\n  \"range_reads_total\": 456,\n  \"range_bytes_saved\": 10737418240,\n  \"cache_hits\": 12000,\n  \"cache_misses\": 3234,\n  \"key_wrap_ops\": 150,\n  \"key_unwrap_ops\": 15000,\n  \"canary_checks\": 240,\n  \"canary_failures\": 0,\n  \"active_multipart\": 0,\n  \"provenance_entries\": 150,\n  \"uptime_seconds\": 86400.0\n}\n```\n\n## Dashboard Endpoints\n\n| Endpoint | Method | Description |\n|----------|--------|-------------|\n| `/dashboard` | GET | Main dashboard UI (HTML) |\n| `/dashboard?prefix=data/` | GET | Browse with prefix filter |\n| `/dashboard/object?key=path/to/file` | GET | Object details (JSON) |\n| `/dashboard/metrics` | GET | All metrics (JSON) |\n\n## Performance Considerations\n\n- **Listing performance**: The dashboard fetches up to 1000 objects per request. For buckets with many objects, use prefix navigation to narrow the scope.\n- **Cache warm-up**: After ARMOR restarts, the cache hit rate will be low until metadata is loaded. The manifest index (if enabled) will warm the cache on startup.\n- **No auth required**: The dashboard is currently accessible to anyone with network access to the admin port. Secure it appropriately in production.\n\n## Troubleshooting\n\n### Dashboard shows \"Failed to list objects\"\n\n1. Check B2 connectivity: `kubectl exec deploy/armor -- curl -s localhost:9001/healthz`\n2. Verify credentials: Check B2 credentials in the `armor-secrets` Secret\n3. Check logs: `kubectl logs -f deploy/armor`\n\n### Can't access dashboard externally\n\n1. Verify Service exists: `kubectl get svc armor`\n2. Check port-forward is running: `kubectl port-forward svc/armor 9001:9001`\n3. For Ingress: Verify Ingress controller is running and DNS is configured\n\n### Cache hit rate is 0%\n\nThis is normal for:\n- Fresh ARMOR deployments (cache not yet warmed)\n- Buckets with poor access locality (random object access)\n- After cache clears (TTL expiration)\n\nThe cache will warm up as objects are accessed. For frequently-accessed objects (e.g., Parquet footers, hot data), you should see 60-90% hit rates during normal operation.\n\n## Future Enhancements\n\nPotential improvements for the dashboard:\n\n- **Historical metrics** - Graph metrics over time using Prometheus/Grafana\n- **Object search** - Full-text search across object keys\n- **Bulk operations** - Select multiple objects for deletion or re-encryption\n- **Key management UI** - Visual interface for key rotation and multi-key configuration (key rotation trigger already implemented)\n- **Upload/download** - Direct file upload and download through the web UI\n- **Real-time updates** - WebSocket updates for live metrics and new objects\n\n## Contributing\n\nThe dashboard is implemented in Go with no external frontend dependencies. grid\n239\t\tRangeBytesSaved string\n240\t\tKeyWrapOps      string\n241\t\tKeyUnwrapOps    string\n242\t}\n243\t\n244\t// Breadcrumb represents a navigation breadcrumb.\n245\ttype Breadcrumb struct {\n246\t\tName string\n247\t\tPath string\n248\t}\n249\t\n250\tfunc (d *Dashboard) buildPageData(result *backend.ListResult, prefix string) PageData {\n251\t\tobjects := make([]ObjectInfo, 0, len(result.CommonPrefixes)+len(result.Objects))\n252\t\tvar encCount, plainCount int\n253\t\tkeyIDSet := make(map[string]struct{})\n254\t\n255\t\t// Add common prefixes (virtual folders) first so they appear at the top.\n256\t\tfor _, cp := range result.CommonPrefixes {\n257\t\t\tobjects = append(objects, ObjectInfo{\n258\t\t\t\tKey:            cp,\n259\t\t\t\tIsFolder:       true,\n260\t\t\t\tPlaintextSizeH: \"—\",\n261\t\t\t})\n262\t\t}\n263\t\n264\t\tfor _, obj := range result.Objects {\n265\t\t\tinfo := ObjectInfo{\n266\t\t\t\tKey:          obj.Key,\n267\t\t\t\tSize:         obj.Size,\n268\t\t\t\tLastModified: obj.LastModified.Format(\"2006-01-02 15:04:05\"),\n269\t\t\t\tContentType:  obj.ContentType,\n270\t\t\t\tETag:         obj.ETag,\n271\t\t\t\tIsFolder:     strings.HasSuffix(obj.Key, \"/\"),\n272\t\t\t}\n273\t\n274\t\t\t// Check if ARMOR-encrypted\n275\t\t\tif obj.IsARMOREncrypted {\n276\t\t\t\tinfo.IsARMOR = true\n277\t\t\t\t// Size is already plaintext size for ARMOR objects\n278\t\t\t\tinfo.PlaintextSize = obj.Size\n279\t\t\t\tinfo.PlaintextSizeH = formatBytes(obj.Size)\n280\t\t\t\t// Extract additional ARMOR metadata\n281\t\t\t\tif armorMeta, ok := backend.ParseARMORMetadata(obj.Metadata); ok {\n282\t\t\t\t\tinfo.KeyID = armorMeta.KeyID\n283\t\t\t\t\tinfo.BlockSize = armorMeta.BlockSize\n284\t\t\t\t}\n285\t\t\t\tif !info.IsFolder {\n286\t\t\t\t\tencCount++\n287\t\t\t\t\tkeyID := info.KeyID\n288\t\t\t\t\tif keyID == \"\" {\n289\t\t\t\t\t\tkeyID = \"default\"\n290\t\t\t\t\t}\n291\t\t\t\t\tkeyIDSet[keyID] = struct{}{}\n292\t\t\t\t}\n293\t\t\t} else {\n294\t\t\t\tinfo.PlaintextSize = obj.Size\n295\t\t\t\tinfo.PlaintextSizeH = formatBytes(obj.Size)\n296\t\t\t\tif !info.IsFolder {\n297\t\t\t\t\tplainCount++\n298\t\t\t\t}\n299\t\t\t}\n300\t\n301\t\t\tobjects = append(objects, info)\n302\t\t}\n303\t\n304\t\t// Build breadcrumbs\n305\t\tbreadcrumbs := []Breadcrumb{{Name: d.bucket, Path: \"\"}}\n306\t\tif prefix != \"\" {\n307\t\t\tparts := strings.Split(strings.TrimSuffix(prefix, \"/\"), \"/\")\n308\t\t\tpath := \"\"\n309\t\t\tfor _, part := range parts {\n310\t\t\t\tif part == \"\" {\n311\t\t\t\t\tcontinue\n312\t\t\t\t}\n313\t\t\t\tpath += part + \"/\"\n314\t\t\t\tbreadcrumbs = append(breadcrumbs, Breadcrumb{Name: part, Path: path})\n315\t\t\t}\n316\t\t}\n317\t\n318\t\t// Get metrics\n319\t\tcacheHits := d.metrics.CacheHitsTotal.String()\n320\t\tcacheMisses := d.metrics.CacheMissesTotal.String()\n321\t\thitRate := \"0%\"\n322\t\tif hits, misses := parseExpvarInt(cacheHits), parseExpvarInt(cacheMisses); hits+misses > 0 {\n323\t\t\trate := float64(hits) / float64(hits+misses) * 100\n324\t\t\thitRate = fmt.Sprintf(\"%.1f%%\", rate)\n325\t\t}\n326\t\n327\t\t// Build sorted key IDs list for the encryption coverage panel\n328\t\tkeyIDs := make([]string, 0, len(keyIDSet))\n329\t\tfor k := range keyIDSet {\n330\t\t\tkeyIDs = append(keyIDs, k)\n331\t\t}\n332\t\tsort.Strings(keyIDs)\n333\t\n334\t\ttotalObjCount := encCount + plainCount\n335\t\tencPct := \"0\"\n336\t\tif totalObjCount > 0 {\n337\t\t\tencPct = fmt.Sprintf(\"%.1f\", float64(encCount)/float64(totalObjCount)*100)\n338\t\t}\n339\t\n340\t\tcanaryStatus, canaryCardClass := d.getCanaryStatus()\n341\t\treturn PageData{\n342\t\t\tBucket:           d.bucket,\n343\t\t\tPrefix:           prefix,\n344\t\t\tObjects:          objects,\n345\t\t\tCacheHits:        cacheHits,\n346\t\t\tCacheMisses:      cacheMisses,\n347\t\t\tCacheHitRate:     hitRate,\n348\t\t\tUptime:           formatUptime(time.Since(d.metrics.StartTime())),\n349\t\t\tRequests:         d.metrics.RequestsTotal.String(),\n350\t\t\tBytesUp:          formatBytes(parseExpvarInt(d.metrics.BytesUploaded.String())),\n351\t\t\tBytesDown:        formatBytes(parseExpvarInt(d.metrics.BytesDownloaded.String())),\n352\t\t\tCanaryStatus:     canaryStatus,\n353\t\t\tCanaryCardClass:  canaryCardClass,\n354\t\t\tBreadcrumbs:      breadcrumbs,\n355\t\t\tEncryptedCount:   encCount,\n356\t\t\tPlaintextCount:   plainCount,\n357\t\t\tTotalObjectCount: totalObjCount,\n358\t\t\tKeyIDs:           keyIDs,\n359\t\t\tEncryptedPct:     encPct,\n360\t\t\tRangeBytesSaved:  formatBytes(parseExpvarInt(d.metrics.RangeBytesSavedTotal.String())),\n361\t\t\tKeyWrapOps:       d.metrics.KeyWrapOpsTotal.String(),\n362\t\t\tKeyUnwrapOps:     d.metrics.KeyUnwrapOpsTotal.String(),\n363\t\t}\n364\t}\n365\t\n366\t// getCanaryStatus returns (status string, CSS card class).\n367\t// CSS class is \"healthy\", \"unhealthy\", or \"\" for not-yet-started.\n368\tfunc (d *Dashboard) getCanaryStatus() (string, string) {\n369\t\t// Use Value() to get the raw string; String() returns JSON-quoted form.\n370\t\tlastCheck := \"healthy\"\n384\t}\n385\t\n386\t// ObjectDetailHandler returns details for a specific object.\n387\tfunc (d *Dashboard) ObjectDetailHandler() http.HandlerFunc {\n388\t\treturn *Dashboard) objectDetailHandlerImpl() http.HandlerFunc {\n398\t\treturn func(w http.ResponseWriter, r *http.Request) {\n399\t\t\tkey := r.URL.Query().Get(\"key\")\n400\t\t\tif key == \"\" {\n401\t\t\t\thttp.Error(w, \"key parameter required\", http.StatusBadRequest)\n402\t\t\t\treturn\n403\t\t\t}\n404\t\n405\t\t\tctx, cancel := context.WithTimeout(r.Context(),    info.Size,\n418\t\t\t\t\"content_type\":  info.ContentType,\n419\t\t\t\t\"etag\":          info.ETag,\n420\t\t\t\t\"last_modified\": \"application/json\")\n439\t\t\tjson.NewEncoder(w).Encode(detail)\n440\t\t}\n441\t}\n442\t\n443\t// MetricsHandler returns metrics in JSON format.\n444\tfunc (d *Dashboard) MetricsHandler() {\n461\t\t\t\tcacheHitRatePct = float64(cacheHits) / float64(cacheHits+cacheMisses) * 100\n462\t\t\t}\n463\t\t\tdata := map[string]interface{}{\n464\t\t\t\t\"requests_total\":        parseExpvarInt(m.RequestsTotal.String()),\n465\t\t\t\t\"requests_in_flight\":    parseExpvarInt(m.RequestsInFlight.String()),\n466\t\t\t\t\"bytes_uploaded\": parseExpvarInt(m.ProvenanceEntriesTotal.String()),\n480\t\t\t\t\"uptime_seconds\":        time.Since(m.StartTime()).Seconds(),\n481\t\t\t\t\"uptime_formatted\": KeyRotateHandler handles key rotation requests.\n489\t// It generates a new MEK and calls the admin API to perform rotation.\n490\tfunc (d *Dashboard) KeyRotateHandler(adminClient *http.Client, adminURL string) http.HandlerFunc {\n491\t\treturn d.keyRotateHandlerImpl(adminClient, adminURL)\n492\t}\n493\t\n494\t// KeyRotateHandlerWithAuth handles key rotation requests with authentication.\n495\tfunc (d *Dashboard) KeyRotateHandlerWithAuth(adminClient *http.Client, adminURL string) http.HandlerFunc {\n496\t\treturn d.auth.Wrap(d.keyRotateHandlerImpl(adminClient, adminURL))\n497\t}\n498\t\n499\t// keyRotateHandlerImpl is the actual implementation of the key rotation handler.\n500\tfunc (d *Dashboard) keyRotateHandlerImpl(adminClient *http.Client, adminURL string) http.HandlerFunc {\n501\t\treturn func(w http.ResponseWriter, r *http.Request) {\n502\t\t\tif r.Method != http.MethodPost {\n503\t\t\t\thttp.Error(w, \"Method not allowed\", http.StatusMethodNotAllowed)\n504\t\t\t\treturn\n505\t\t\t}\n506\t\n507\t\t\t// Generate a new MEK (32 random bytes)\n508\t\t\tnewMEK := make([]byte, 32)\n509\t\t\tif _, err := rand.Read(newMEK); err != nil {\n510\t\t\t\thttp.Error(w, fmt.Sprintf(\"Failed to generate new MEK: %v\", err), http.StatusInternalServerError)\n511\t\t\t\treturn\n512\t\t\t}\n513\t\n514\t\t\t// Call the admin API's rotate endpoint\n515\t\t\trotateURL := adminURL\n516\t\t\tif rotateURL == \"\" {\n517\t\t\t\trotateURL = \"http://127.0.0.1:9001/admin/key/rotate\"\n518\t\t\t}\n519\t\n520\t\t\t// Send the new MEK as hex-encoded string\n521\t\t\tmekHex := hex.EncodeToString(newMEK)\n522\t\t\treq, err := http.NewRequestWithContext(r.Context(), http.MethodPost, rotateURL, strings.NewReader(mekHex))\n523\t\t\tif err != nil {\n524\t\t\t\thttp.Error(w, fmt.Sprintf(\"Failed to create request: %v\", err), http.StatusInternalServerError)\n525\t\t\t\treturn\n526\t\t\t}\n527\t\t\treq.Header.Set(\"Content-Type\", \"text/plain\")\n528\t\n529\t\t\tresp, err := adminClient.Do(req)\n530\t\t\tif err != nil {\n531\t\t\t\thttp.Error(w, fmt.Sprintf(\"Failed to call admin API: %v\", err), http.StatusBadGateway)\n532\t\t\t\treturn\n533\t\t\t}\n534\t\t\tdefer resp.Body.Close()\n535\t\n536\t\t\t// Copy response headers and body\n537\t\t\tfor k, v := range resp.Header {\n538\t\t\t\tw.Header()[k] = v\n539\t\t\t}\n540\t\t\tw.WriteHeader(resp.StatusCode)\n541\t\t\tio.Copy(w, resp.Body)\n542\t\t}\n543\t}\n544\t\n545\t// EncryptionStatsResponse holds encryption statistics for a bucket listing.\n546\ttype EncryptionStatsResponse struct {\n547\t\tEncryptedCount  int            `json:\"encrypted_count\"`\n548\t\tPlaintextCount  int            `json:\"plaintext_count\"`\n549\t\tTotalCount      int            `json:\"total_count\"`\n550\t\tEncryptedBytes  int64          `json:\"encrypted_bytes\"`\n551\t\tPlaintextBytes  int64          `json:\"plaintext_bytes\"`\n552\t\tKeyIDs          []string       `json:\"key_ids\"`\n553\t\tKeyUsage        map[string]int `json:\"key_usage\"`\n554\t\tCoveragePercent float64        `json:\"coverage_percent\"`\n555\t}\n556\t\n557\t// EncryptionStatsHandler returns encryption statistics for the bucket.\n558\tfunc (d *Dashboard) EncryptionStatsHandler() http.HandlerFunc {\n559\t\treturn d.encryptionStatsHandlerImpl()\n560\t}\n561\t\n562\t// EncryptionStatsHandlerWithAuth returns the encryption stats handler with authentication.\n563\tfunc (d *Dashboard) EncryptionStatsHandlerWithAuth() http.HandlerFunc {\n564\t\treturn d.auth.Wrap(d.encryptionStatsHandlerImpl())\n565\t}\n566\t\n567\tfunc (d *Dashboard) encryptionStatsHandlerImpl() http.HandlerFunc {\n568\t\treturn func(w http.ResponseWriter, r *http.Request) {\n569\t\t\tprefix := r.URL.Query().Get(\"prefix\")\n570\t\n571\t\t\tctx, cancel := context.WithTimeout(r.Context(), 30*time.Second)\n572\t\t\tdefer cancel()\n573\t\n574\t\t\t// Use no delimiter to list all objects (not just top-level) for accurate stats\n575\t\t\tresult, err := d.backend.List(ctx, d.bucket, prefix, \"\", \"\", 1000)\n576\t\t\tif err != nil {\n577\t\t\t\thttp.Error(w, fmt.Sprintf(\"Failed to list objects: %v\", err), http.StatusInternalServerError)\n578\t\t\t\treturn\n579\t\t\t}\n580\t\n581\t\t\tstats := EncryptionStatsResponse{\n582\t\t\t\tKeyUsage: make(map[string]int),\n583\t\t\t}\n584\t\n585\t\t\tfor _, obj := range result.Objects {\n586\t\t\t\tif strings.HasSuffix(obj.Key, \"/\") {\n587\t\t\t\t\tcontinue\n588\t\t\t\t}\n589\t\t\t\tstats.TotalCount++\n590\t\t\t\tif obj.IsARMOREncrypted {\n591\t\t\t\t\tstats.EncryptedCount++\n592\t\t\t\t\tstats.EncryptedBytes += obj.Size\n593\t\t\t\t\tkeyID := \"default\"\n594\t\t\t\t\tif armorMeta, ok := backend.ParseARMORMetadata(obj.Metadata); ok && armorMeta.KeyID != \"\" {\n595\t\t\t\t\t\tkeyID = armorMeta.KeyID\n596\t\t\t\t\t}\n597\t\t\t\t\tstats.KeyUsage[keyID]++\n598\t\t\t\t} else {\n599\t\t\t\t\tstats.PlaintextCount++\n600\t\t\t\t\tstats.PlaintextBytes += obj.Size\n601\t\t\t\t}\n602\t\t\t}\n603\t\n604\t\t\tfor k := range stats.KeyUsage {\n605\t\t\t\tstats.KeyIDs = append(stats.KeyIDs, k)\n606\t\t\t}\n607\t\t\tsort.Strings(stats.KeyIDs)\n608\t\n609\t\t\tif stats.TotalCount > 0 {\n610\t\t\t\tstats.CoveragePercent = float64(stats.EncryptedCount) / float64(stats.TotalCount) * 100\n611\t\t\t}\n612\t\n613\t\t\tw.Header().Set(\"Content-Type\", \"application/json\")\n614\t\t\tjson.NewEncoder(w).Encode(stats)\n615\t\t}\n616\t}\n617\t\n618\t// Helper functions\n619\t\n620\tfunc parseExpvarInt(s string) int64 {\n621\t\tn, _ := strconv.ParseInt(s, 10, 64)\n622\t\treturn n\n623\t}\n624\t\n625\tfunc formatBytes(n int64) string {\n626\t\tif n < 1024 {\n627\t\t\treturn fmt.Sprintf(\"%d B\", n)\n628\t\t}\n629\t\tif n < 1024*1024 {\n630\t\t\treturn fmt.Sprintf(\"%.1f KB\", float64(n)/1024)\n631\t\t}\n632\t\tif n < 1024*1024*1024 {\n633\t\t\treturn fmt.Sprintf(\"%.1f MB\", float64(n)/(1024*1024))\n634\t\t}\n635\t\treturn fmt.Sprintf(\"%.1f GB\", float64(n)/(1024*1024*1024))\n636\t}\n637\t\n638\tfunc formatUptime(d time.Duration) string {\n639\t\td = d.Round(time.Second)\n640\t\th := d / time.Hour\n641\t\td -= h * time.Hour\n642\t\tm := d / time.Minute\n643\t\td -= m * time.Minute\n644\t\ts := d / time.Second\n645\t\treturn fmt.Sprintf(\"%dh %dm %ds\", h, m, s)\n646\t}\n647\t\n648\t// The HTML template for the dashboard\n649\tconst dashboardHTML = `<!DOCTYPE html>\n650\t<html lang=\"en\">\n651\t<head>\n652\t    <meta sets the WWW-Authenticate header.\nfunc (a *AuthMiddleware) Authenticate(w http.ResponseWriter, r *http.Request) bool {\n\t// No auth configured - allow all\n\tif a.user == \"\" && a.token == \"\" {\n\t\treturn true\n\t}\n\n\t// Check Bearer token first\n\tif a.token != \"\" {\n\t\tauthHeader := r.Header.Get(\"Authorization\")\n\t\tif strings.HasPrefix(authHeader, \"Bearer \") {\n\t\t\ttoken := strings.TrimPrefix(authHeader, \"Bearer \")\n\t\t\tif token == a.token {\n\t\t\t\treturn true\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\t// Check HTTP Basic Auth\n\tif a.user != \"\" && a.pass != \"\" {\n\t\tauthHeader := r.Header.Get(\"Authorization\")\n\t\tif strings.HasPrefix(authHeader, \"Basic \") {\n\t\t\tencodedCreds := strings.TrimPrefix(authHeader, \"Basic \")\n\t\t\tdecodedCreds, err := base64.StdEncoding.DecodeString(encodedCreds)\n\t\t\tif err == nil {\n\t\t\t\tcreds := strings.SplitN(string(decodedCreds), \":\", 2)\n\t\t\t\tif len(creds) == 2 && creds[0] == a.user && creds[1] == a.pass {\n\t\t\t\t\treturn true\n\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\t// Authentication failed - set WWW-Authenticate header\n\tw.Header().Set(\"WWW-Authenticate\", `Basic realm=\"ARMOR Dashboard\"`)\n\thttp.Error(w, \"Unauthorized\", http.StatusUnauthorized)\n\treturn false\n}\n\n// Wrap wraps a handler with authentication middleware.\nfunc (a *AuthMiddleware) Wrap(h http.HandlerFunc) http.HandlerFunc {\n\treturn func(w http.ResponseWriter, r *http.Request) {\n\t\tif !a.Authenticate(w, r) {\n\t\t\treturn\n\t\t}\n\t\th(w, r)\n\t}\n}\n\n// Dashboard provides the web dashboard handlers.\ntype Dashboard struct {\n\tbackend  backend.Backend\n\tbucket   string\n\tmetrics  *metrics.Metrics\n\ttemplate *template.Template\n\tauth     *AuthMiddleware\n}\n\n// New creates a new Dashboard.\nfunc New(b backend.Backend, bucket string, m *metrics.Metrics) *Dashboard {\n\treturn NewWithAuth(b, bucket, m, \"\", \"\", \"\")\n}\n\n// NewWithAuth creates a new Dashboard with authentication.\nfunc NewWithAuth(b backend.Backend, bucket string, m *metrics.Metrics, user, pass, token string) *Dashboard {\n\td := &Dashboard{\n\t\tbackend: b,\n\t\tbucket:  bucket,\n\t\tmetrics: m,\n\t\tauth:    NewAuthMiddleware(user, pass, token),\n\t}\n\td.template = template.Must(template.New(\"dashboard\").Parse(dashboardHTML))\n\treturn d\n}\n\n// KeyRotateStatusHandler returns the current key rotation status.\n// This polls the rotation state file from B2 for progress information.\nfunc (d *Dashboard) KeyRotateStatusHandler() http.HandlerFunc {\n\treturn d.keyRotateStatusHandlerImpl()\n}\n\n// KeyRotateStatusHandlerWithAuth returns the key rotation status handler with authentication.\nfunc (d *Dashboard) KeyRotateStatusHandlerWithAuth() http.HandlerFunc {\n\treturn d.auth.Wrap(d.keyRotateStatusHandlerImpl())\n}\n\n// keyRotateStatusHandlerImpl is the actual implementation of the key rotation status handler.\nfunc (d *Dashboard) keyRotateStatusHandlerImpl() http.HandlerFunc {\n\treturn func(w http.ResponseWriter, r *http.Request) {\n\t\tif r.Method != http.MethodGet {\n\t\t\thttp.Error(w, \"Method not allowed\", http.StatusMethodNotAllowed)\n\t\t\treturn\n\t\t}\n\n\t\tctx, cancel := context.WithTimeout(r.Context(), 10*time.Second)\n\t\tdefer cancel()\n\n\t\t// Try to read the rotation state file\n\t\tstatePath := \".armor/rotation-state.json\"\n\t\treader, _, err := d.backend.GetDirect(ctx, d.bucket, statePath)\n\t\tif err != nil {\n\t\t\t// No rotation state file means no rotation in progress\n\t\t\tw.Header().Set(\"Content-Type\", \"application/json\")\n\t\t\tjson.NewEncoder(w).Encode(map[string]interface{}{\n\t\t\t\t\"status\": \"none\",\n\t\t\t\t\"message\": \"No rotation in progress\",\n\t\t\t})\n\t\t\treturn\n\t\t}\n\t\tdefer reader.Close()\n\n\t\tdata, err := io.ReadAll(reader)\n\t\tif err != nil {\n\t\t\thttp.Error(w, fmt.Sprintf(\"Failed to read state: %v\", err), http.StatusInternalServerError)\n\t\t\treturn\n\t\t}\n\n\t\t// Return the raw state file content\n\t\tw.Header().Set(\"Content-Type\", \"application/json\")\n\t\tw.Write(data)\n\t}\n}\n\n// Handler returns the main dashboard handler.\nfunc (d *Dashboard) Handler() http.HandlerFunc {\n\treturn d.handlerImpl()\n}\n\n// HandlerWithAuth returns the main dashboard handler with authentication.\nfunc (d *Dashboard) HandlerWithAuth() http.HandlerFunc {\n\treturn d.auth.Wrap(d.handlerImpl())\n}\n\n// handlerImpl is the actual implementation of the main dashboard handler.\nfunc (d *Dashboard) handlerImpl() http.HandlerFunc {\n\treturn func(w http.ResponseWriter, r *http.Request) {\n\t\t// Get prefix from query\n\t\tprefix := r.URL.Query().Get(\"prefix\")\n\n\t\t// List objects\n\t\tctx, cancel := context.WithTimeout(r.Context(), 30*time.Second)\n\t\tdefer cancel()\n\n\t\tresult, err := d.backend.List(ctx, d.bucket, prefix, \"/\", \"\", 1000)\n\t\tif err != nil {\n\t\t\thttp.Error(w, fmt.Sprintf(\"Failed to list objects: %v\", err), http.StatusInternalServerError)\n\t\t\treturn\n\t\t}\n\n\t\t// Build page data\n\t\tdata := d.buildPageData(result, prefix)\n\n\t\tw.Header().Set(\"Content-Type\", \"text/html; charset=utf-8\")\n\t\tif err := d.template.Execute(w, data); err != nil {\n\t\t\thttp.Error(w, fmt.Sprintf(\"Template error: %v\", err), http.StatusInternalServerError)\n\t\t\treturn\n\t\t}\n\t}\n}\n\n// ObjectInfo represents an object in the dashboard.\ntype ObjectInfo struct {\n\tKey            string\n\tSize           int64\n\tPlaintextSize  int64\n\tLastModified   string\n\tIsARMOR        bool\n\tContentType    string\n\tETag           string\n\tKeyID          string\n\tBlockSize      int\n\tIsFolder       bool\n\tPlaintextSizeH string\n}\n\n// PageData holds data for the dashboard template.\ntype PageData struct {\n\tBucket          string\n\tPrefix          string\n\tObjects         []ObjectInfo\n\tCacheHits       string\n\tCacheMisses     string\n\tCacheHitRate    string\n\tUptime          string\n\tRequests        string\n\tBytesUp         string\n\tBytesDown       string\n\tCanaryStatus    string\n\tCanaryCardClass string // \"healthy\", \"unhealthy\", or \"\" for not-yet-started\n\tBreadcrumbs     []Breadcrumb\n\t// Encryption statistics for the current listing\n\tEncryptedCount   int\n\tPlaintextCount   int\n\tTotalObjectCount int     // EncryptedCount + PlaintextCount (excludes folders)\n\tKeyIDs           []string\n\tEncryptedPct     string  // e.g. \"75.0\" — used as CSS width and display value\n\t// Additional metrics exposed in the stats grid\n\tRangeBytesSaved string\n\tKeyWrapOps      string\n\tKeyUnwrapOps    string\n}\n\n// Breadcrumb represents a navigation breadcrumb.\ntype Breadcrumb struct {\n\tName string\n\tPath string\n}\n\nfunc (d *Dashboard) buildPageData(result *backend.ListResult, prefix string) PageData {\n\tobjects := make([]ObjectInfo, 0, len(result.CommonPrefixes)+len(result.Objects))\n\tvar encCount, plainCount int\n\tkeyIDSet := make(map[string]struct{})\n\n\t// Add common prefixes (virtual folders) first so they appear at the top.\n\tfor _, cp := range result.CommonPrefixes {\n\t\tobjects = append(objects, ObjectInfo{\n\t\t\tKey:            cp,\n\t\t\tIsFolder:       true,\n\t\t\tPlaintextSizeH: \"—\",\n\t\t})\n\t}\n\n\tfor _, obj := range result.Objects {\n\t\tinfo := ObjectInfo{\n\t\t\tKey:          obj.Key,\n\t\t\tSize:         obj.Size,\n\t\t\tLastModified: obj.LastModified.Format(\"2006-01-02 15:04:05\"),\n\t\t\tContentType:  obj.ContentType,\n\t\t\tETag:         obj.ETag,\n\t\t\tIsFolder:     strings.HasSuffix(obj.Key, \"/\"),\n\t\t}\n\n\t\t// Check if ARMOR-encrypted\n\t\tif obj.IsARMOREncrypted {\n\t\t\tinfo.IsARMOR = true\n\t\t\t// Size is already plaintext size for ARMOR objects\n\t\t\tinfo.PlaintextSize = obj.Size\n\t\t\tinfo.PlaintextSizeH = formatBytes(obj.Size)\n\t\t\t// Extract additional ARMOR metadata\n\t\t\tif armorMeta, ok := backend.ParseARMORMetadata(obj.Metadata); ok {\n\t\t\t\tinfo.KeyID = armorMeta.KeyID\n\t\t\t\tinfo.BlockSize = armorMeta.BlockSize\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t\tif !info.IsFolder {\n\t\t\t\tencCount++\n\t\t\t\tkeyID := info.KeyID\n\t\t\t\tif keyID == \"\" {\n\t\t\t\t\tkeyID = \"default\"\n\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t\tkeyIDSet[keyID] = struct{}{}\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t} else {\n\t\t\tinfo.PlaintextSize = obj.Size\n\t\t\tinfo.PlaintextSizeH = formatBytes(obj.Size)\n\t\t\tif !info.IsFolder {\n\t\t\t\tplainCount++\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t}\n\n\t\tobjects = append(objects, info)\n\t}\n\n\t// Build breadcrumbs\n\tbreadcrumbs := []Breadcrumb{{Name: d.bucket, Path: \"\"}}\n\tif prefix != \"\" {\n\t\tparts := strings.Split(strings.TrimSuffix(prefix, \"/\"), \"/\")\n\t\tpath := \"\"\n\t\tfor _, part := range parts {\n\t\t\tif part == \"\" {\n\t\t\t\tcontinue\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t\tpath += part + \"/\"\n\t\t\tbreadcrumbs = append(breadcrumbs, Breadcrumb{Name: part, Path: path})\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\t// Get metrics\n\tcacheHits := d.metrics.CacheHitsTotal.String()\n\tcacheMisses := d.metrics.CacheMissesTotal.String()\n\thitRate := \"0%\"\n\tif hits, misses := parseExpvarInt(cacheHits), parseExpvarInt(cacheMisses); hits+misses > 0 {\n\t\trate := float64(hits) / float64(hits+misses) * 100\n\t\thitRate = fmt.Sprintf(\"%.1f%%\", rate)\n\t}\n\n\t// Build sorted key IDs list for the encryption coverage panel\n\tkeyIDs := make([]string, 0, len(keyIDSet))\n\tfor k := range keyIDSet {\n\t\tkeyIDs = append(keyIDs, k)\n\t}\n\tsort.Strings(keyIDs)\n\n\ttotalObjCount := encCount + plainCount\n\tencPct := \"0\"\n\tif totalObjCount > 0 {\n\t\tencPct = fmt.Sprintf(\"%.1f\", float64(encCount)/float64(totalObjCount)*100)\n\t}\n\n\tcanaryStatus, canaryCardClass := d.getCanaryStatus()\n\treturn PageData{\n\t\tBucket:           d.bucket,\n\t\tPrefix:           prefix,\n\t\tObjects:          objects,\n\t\tCacheHits:        cacheHits,\n\t\tCacheMisses:      cacheMisses,\n\t\tCacheHitRate:     hitRate,\n\t\tUptime:           formatUptime(time.Since(d.metrics.StartTime())),\n\t\tRequests:         d.metrics.RequestsTotal.String(),\n\t\tBytesUp:          formatBytes(parseExpvarInt(d.metrics.BytesUploaded.String())),\n\t\tBytesDown:        formatBytes(parseExpvarInt(d.metrics.BytesDownloaded.String())),\n\t\tCanaryStatus:     canaryStatus,\n\t\tCanaryCardClass:  canaryCardClass,\n\t\tBreadcrumbs:      breadcrumbs,\n\t\tEncryptedCount:   encCount,\n\t\tPlaintextCount:   plainCount,\n\t\tTotalObjectCount: totalObjCount,\n\t\tKeyIDs:           keyIDs,\n\t\tEncryptedPct:     encPct,\n\t\tRangeBytesSaved:  formatBytes(parseExpvarInt(d.metrics.RangeBytesSavedTotal.String())),\n\t\tKeyWrapOps:       d.metrics.KeyWrapOpsTotal.String(),\n\t\tKeyUnwrapOps:     d.metrics.KeyUnwrapOpsTotal.String(),\n\t}\n}\n\n// getCanaryStatus returns (status string, CSS card class).\n// CSS class is \"healthy\", \"unhealthy\", or \"\" for not-yet-started.\nfunc (d *Dashboard) getCanaryStatus() (string, string) {\n\t// Use Value() to get the raw string; String() returns JSON-quoted form.\n\tlastCheck := d.metrics.CanaryLastCheckTime.Value()\n\tfailures := parseExpvarInt(d.metrics.CanaryCheckFailures.String())\n\n\tif failures > 0 {\n\t\terrMsg := d.metrics.CanaryLastCheckError.Value()\n\t\tif errMsg != \"\" {\n\t\t\treturn fmt.Sprintf(\"Unhealthy: %s\", errMsg), \"unhealthy\"\n\t\t}\n\t\treturn fmt.Sprintf(\"Unhealthy (failures: %d)\", failures), \"unhealthy\"\n\t}\n\tif lastCheck == \"\" {\n\t\treturn \"Not started\", \"\"\n\t}\n\treturn fmt.Sprintf(\"Healthy (last: %s)\", lastCheck), \"healthy\"\n}\n\n// ObjectDetailHandler returns details for a specific object.\nfunc (d *Dashboard) ObjectDetailHandler() http.HandlerFunc {\n\treturn d.objectDetailHandlerImpl()\n}\n\n// ObjectDetailHandlerWithAuth returns the object detail handler with authentication.\nfunc (d *Dashboard) ObjectDetailHandlerWithAuth() http.HandlerFunc {\n\treturn d.auth.Wrap(d.objectDetailHandlerImpl())\n}\n\n// objectDetailHandlerImpl is the actual implementation of the object detail handler.\nfunc (d *Dashboard) objectDetailHandlerImpl() http.HandlerFunc {\n\treturn func(w http.ResponseWriter, r *http.Request) {\n\t\tkey := r.URL.Query().Get(\"key\")\n\t\tif key == \"\" {\n\t\t\thttp.Error(w, \"key parameter required\", http.StatusBadRequest)\n\t\t\treturn\n\t\t}\n\n\t\tctx, cancel := context.WithTimeout(r.Context(), 30*time.Second)\n\t\tdefer cancel()\n\n\t\tinfo, err := d.backend.Head(ctx, d.bucket, key)\n\t\tif err != nil {\n\t\t\thttp.Error(w, fmt.Sprintf(\"Failed to get object: %v\", err), http.StatusNotFound)\n\t\t\treturn\n\t\t}\n\n\t\t// Build response\n\t\tdetail := map[string]interface{}{\n\t\t\t\"key\":           key,\n\t\t\t\"size\":          info.Size,\n\t\t\t\"content_type\":  info.ContentType,\n\t\t\t\"etag\":          info.ETag,\n\t\t\t\"last_modified\": info.LastModified.Format(time.RFC3339),\n\t\t\t\"is_armor\":      info.IsARMOREncrypted,\n\t\t}\n\n\t\tif info.IsARMOREncrypted {\n\t\t\tarmorMeta, ok := backend.ParseARMORMetadata(info.Metadata)\n\t\t\tif ok {\n\t\t\t\tdetail[\"armor\"] = map[string]interface{}{\n\t\t\t\t\t\"plaintext_size\": armorMeta.PlaintextSize,\n\t\t\t\t\t\"block_size\":     armorMeta.BlockSize,\n\t\t\t\t\t\"key_id\":         armorMeta.KeyID,\n\t\t\t\t\t\"iv\":             fmt.Sprintf(\"%x\", armorMeta.IV),\n\t\t\t\t\t\"wrapped_dek\":    fmt.Sprintf(\"%x\", armorMeta.WrappedDEK),\n\t\t\t\t\t\"sha256\":         armorMeta.PlaintextSHA,\n\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t}\n\n\t\tw.Header().Set(\"Content-Type\", \"application/json\")\n\t\tjson.NewEncoder(w).Encode(detail)\n\t}\n}\n\n// MetricsHandler returns metrics in JSON format.\nfunc (d *Dashboard) MetricsHandler() http.HandlerFunc {\n\treturn d.metricsHandlerImpl()\n}\n\n// MetricsHandlerWithAuth returns the metrics handler with authentication.\nfunc (d *Dashboard) MetricsHandlerWithAuth() http.HandlerFunc {\n\treturn d.auth.Wrap(d.metricsHandlerImpl())\n}\n\n// metricsHandlerImpl is the actual implementation of the metrics handler.\nfunc (d *Dashboard) metricsHandlerImpl() http.HandlerFunc {\n\treturn func(w http.ResponseWriter, r *http.Request) {\n\t\tm := d.metrics\n\t\tcacheHits := parseExpvarInt(m.CacheHitsTotal.String())\n\t\tcacheMisses := parseExpvarInt(m.CacheMissesTotal.String())\n\t\tvar cacheHitRatePct float64\n\t\tif cacheHits+cacheMisses > 0 {\n\t\t\tcacheHitRatePct = float64(cacheHits) / float64(cacheHits+cacheMisses) * 100\n\t\t}\n\t\tdata := map[string]interface{}{\n\t\t\t\"requests_total\":        parseExpvarInt(m.RequestsTotal.String()),\n\t\t\t\"requests_in_flight\":    parseExpvarInt(m.RequestsInFlight.String()),\n\t\t\t\"bytes_uploaded\":        parseExpvarInt(m.BytesUploaded.String()),\n\t\t\t\"bytes_downloaded\":      parseExpvarInt(m.BytesDownloaded.String()),\n\t\t\t\"bytes_fetched_from_b2\": parseExpvarInt(m.BytesFetchedFromB2.String()),\n\t\t\t\"range_reads_total\":     parseExpvarInt(m.RangeReadsTotal.String()),\n\t\t\t\"range_bytes_saved\":     parseExpvarInt(m.RangeBytesSavedTotal.String()),\n\t\t\t\"cache_hits\":            cacheHits,\n\t\t\t\"cache_misses\":          cacheMisses,\n\t\t\t\"cache_hit_rate_pct\":    cacheHitRatePct,\n\t\t\t\"key_wrap_ops\":          parseExpvarInt(m.KeyWrapOpsTotal.String()),\n\t\t\t\"key_unwrap_ops\":        parseExpvarInt(m.KeyUnwrapOpsTotal.String()),\n\t\t\t\"canary_checks\":         parseExpvarInt(m.CanaryChecksTotal.String()),\n\t\t\t\"canary_failures\":       parseExpvarInt(m.CanaryCheckFailures.String()),\n\t\t\t\"active_multipart\":      parseExpvarInt(m.ActiveMultipartUploads.String()),\n\t\t\t\"provenance_entries\":    parseExpvarInt(m.ProvenanceEntriesTotal.String()),\n\t\t\t\"uptime_seconds\":        time.Since(m.StartTime()).Seconds(),\n\t\t\t\"uptime_formatted\":      formatUptime(time.Since(m.StartTime())),\n\t\t}\n\t\tw.Header().Set(\"Content-Type\", \"application/json\")\n\t\tjson.NewEncoder(w).Encode(data)\n\t}\n}\n\n// KeyRotateHandler handles key rotation requests.\n// It generates a new MEK and calls the admin API to perform rotation.\nfunc (d *Dashboard) KeyRotateHandler(adminClient *http.Client, adminURL string) http.HandlerFunc {\n\treturn d.keyRotateHandlerImpl(adminClient, adminURL)\n}\n\n// KeyRotateHandlerWithAuth handles key rotation requests with authentication.\nfunc (d *Dashboard) KeyRotateHandlerWithAuth(adminClient *http.Client, adminURL string) http.HandlerFunc {\n\treturn d.auth.Wrap(d.keyRotateHandlerImpl(adminClient, adminURL))\n}\n\n// keyRotateHandlerImpl is the actual implementation of the key rotation handler.\nfunc (d *Dashboard) keyRotateHandlerImpl(adminClient *http.Client, adminURL string) http.HandlerFunc {\n\treturn func(w http.ResponseWriter, r *http.Request) {\n\t\tif r.Method != http.MethodPost {\n\t\t\thttp.Error(w, \"Method not allowed\", http.StatusMethodNotAllowed)\n\t\t\treturn\n\t\t}\n\n\t\t// Generate a new MEK (32 random bytes)\n\t\tnewMEK := make([]byte, 32)\n\t\tif _, err := rand.Read(newMEK); err != nil {\n\t\t\thttp.Error(w, fmt.Sprintf(\"Failed to generate new MEK: %v\", err), http.StatusInternalServerError)\n\t\t\treturn\n\t\t}\n\n\t\t// Call the admin API's rotate endpoint\n\t\trotateURL := adminURL\n\t\tif rotateURL == \"\" {\n\t\t\trotateURL = \"http://127.0.0.1:9001/admin/key/rotate\"\n\t\t}\n\n\t\t// Send the new MEK as hex-encoded string\n\t\tmekHex := hex.EncodeToString(newMEK)\n\t\treq, err := http.NewRequestWithContext(r.Context(), http.MethodPost, rotateURL, strings.NewReader(mekHex))\n\t\tif err != nil {\n\t\t\thttp.Error(w, fmt.Sprintf(\"Failed to create request: %v\", err), http.StatusInternalServerError)\n\t\t\treturn\n\t\t}\n\t\treq.Header.Set(\"Content-Type\", \"text/plain\")\n\n\t\tresp, err := adminClient.Do(req)\n\t\tif err != nil {\n\t\t\thttp.Error(w, fmt.Sprintf(\"Failed to call admin API: %v\", err), http.StatusBadGateway)\n\t\t\treturn\n\t\t}\n\t\tdefer resp.Body.Close()\n\n\t\t// Copy response headers and body\n\t\tfor k, v := range resp.Header {\n\t\t\tw.Header()[k] = v\n\t\t}\n\t\tw.WriteHeader(resp.StatusCode)\n\t\tio.Copy(w, resp.Body)\n\t}\n}\n\n// EncryptionStatsResponse holds encryption statistics for a bucket listing.\ntype EncryptionStatsResponse struct {\n\tEncryptedCount  int            `json:\"encrypted_count\"`\n\tPlaintextCount  int            `json:\"plaintext_count\"`\n\tTotalCount      int            `json:\"total_count\"`\n\tEncryptedBytes  int64          `json:\"encrypted_bytes\"`\n\tPlaintextBytes  int64          `json:\"plaintext_bytes\"`\n\tKeyIDs          []string       `json:\"key_ids\"`\n\tKeyUsage        map[string]int `json:\"key_usage\"`\n\tCoveragePercent float64        `json:\"coverage_percent\"`\n}\n\n// EncryptionStatsHandler returns encryption statistics for the bucket.\nfunc (d *Dashboard) EncryptionStatsHandler() http.HandlerFunc {\n\treturn d.encryptionStatsHandlerImpl()\n}\n\n// EncryptionStatsHandlerWithAuth returns the encryption stats handler with authentication.\nfunc (d *Dashboard) EncryptionStatsHandlerWithAuth() http.HandlerFunc {\n\treturn d.auth.Wrap(d.encryptionStatsHandlerImpl())\n}\n\nfunc (d *Dashboard) encryptionStatsHandlerImpl() http.HandlerFunc {\n\treturn func(w http.ResponseWriter, r *http.Request) {\n\t\tprefix := r.URL.Query().Get(\"prefix\")\n\n\t\tctx, cancel := context.WithTimeout(r.Context(), 30*time.Second)\n\t\tdefer cancel()\n\n\t\t// Use no delimiter to list all objects (not just top-level) for accurate stats\n\t\tresult, err := d.backend.List(ctx, d.bucket, prefix, \"\", \"\", 1000)\n\t\tif err != nil {\n\t\t\thttp.Error(w, fmt.Sprintf(\"Failed to list objects: %v\", err), http.StatusInternalServerError)\n\t\t\treturn\n\t\t}\n\n\t\tstats := EncryptionStatsResponse{\n\t\t\tKeyUsage: make(map[string]int),\n\t\t}\n\n\t\tfor _, obj := range result.Objects {\n\t\t\tif strings.HasSuffix(obj.Key, \"/\") {\n\t\t\t\tcontinue\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t\tstats.TotalCount++\n\t\t\tif obj.IsARMOREncrypted {\n\t\t\t\tstats.EncryptedCount++\n\t\t\t\tstats.EncryptedBytes += obj.Size\n\t\t\t\tkeyID := \"default\"\n\t\t\t\tif armorMeta, ok := backend.ParseARMORMetadata(obj.Metadata); ok && armorMeta.KeyID != \"\" {\n\t\t\t\t\tkeyID = armorMeta.KeyID\n\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t\tstats.KeyUsage[keyID]++\n\t\t\t} else {\n\t\t\t\tstats.PlaintextCount++\n\t\t\t\tstats.PlaintextBytes += obj.Size\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t}\n\n\t\tfor k := range stats.KeyUsage {\n\t\t\tstats.KeyIDs = append(stats.KeyIDs, k)\n\t\t}\n\t\tsort.Strings(stats.KeyIDs)\n\n\t\tif stats.TotalCount > 0 {\n\t\t\tstats.CoveragePercent = float64(stats.EncryptedCount) / float64(stats.TotalCount) * 100\n\t\t}\n\n\t\tw.Header().Set(\"Content-Type\", \"application/json\")\n\t\tjson.NewEncoder(w).Encode(stats)\n\t}\n}\n\n// Helper functions\n\nfunc parseExpvarInt(s string) int64 {\n\tn, _ := strconv.ParseInt(s, 10, 64)\n\treturn n\n}\n\nfunc formatBytes(n int64) string {\n\tif n < 1024 {\n\t\treturn fmt.Sprintf(\"%d B\", n)\n\t}\n\tif n < 1024*1024 {\n\t\treturn fmt.Sprintf(\"%.1f KB\", float64(n)/1024)\n\t}\n\tif n < 1024*1024*1024 {\n\t\treturn fmt.Sprintf(\"%.1f MB\", float64(n)/(1024*1024))\n\t}\n\treturn fmt.Sprintf(\"%.1f GB\", := backend.NewFooterCache(cfg.CacheMaxEntries, cfg.CacheTTL)\n\n\t// Create list cache (nil when TTL is 0, meaning disabled)\n\tvar listCache *backend.ListCache\n\tif cfg.ListCacheTTL > 0 keymanager.New(cfg.MEK, cfg.NamedKeys, routes)\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\treturn nil, fmt.Errorf(\"failed to create key manager: %w\", err)\n\t}\n\n\t// Create canary monitor\n\tcanaryMonitor := client (for B2 native API key management)\n\t// Uses the same B2 credentials as the S3 backend\n\tvar b2keysClient *b2keys.Client\n\tif cfg.Bucket != \"\" {\n\t\t// Bucket-scoped configuration: application key is restricted to a single bucket\n\t\t// and cannot call account-level B2 API endpoints (like b2_authorize_account).\n\t\t// Key management is unavailable in this mode, which is expected and intentional.\n\t\tlogger.Info(\"B2 key management disabled (application key is bucket-scoped)\")\n\t} else {\n\t\t// No bucket restriction: attempt to create B2 keys client for account-level operations\n\t\t// Extract account ID from the key ID (B2 key IDs are in format accountIdKeyId)\n\t\t// The account ID is the first 12 characters\n\t\taccountID := cfg.B2AccessKeyID\n\t\tif len(accountID) > 12 {\n\t\t\taccountID = accountID[:12]\n\t\t}\n\t\tb2keysClient, err = b2keys.NewClient(context.Background(), accountID, cfg.B2SecretAccessKey)\n\t\tif err cfg.ManifestEnabled {\n\t\tmanifestIdx = manifest.New()\n\t\t// ListRaw bypasses the .armor/ filter so manifest keys are discoverable.\n\t\tlister := func(ctx context.Context, prefix, token string) ([]string, string, error) {\n\t\t\tresult, lerr := b2Backend.ListRaw(ctx, cfg.Bucket, prefix, \"\", token, 1000)\n\t\t\tif lerr != nil {\n\t\t\t\treturn nil, \"\", lerr\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t\tkeys := make([]string, len(result.Objects))\n\t\t\tfor i, obj := range result.Objects {\n\t\t\t\tkeys[i] = obj.Key\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t\treturn keys, result.NextToken, nil\n\t\t}\n\t\t// Fetch snapshot and delta blobs via Cloudflare for free egress and edge\n\t\t// caching. Fall back to direct B2 if no Cloudflare domain is configured.\n\t\tfetcher := func(ctx context.Context, key string) ([]byte, error) {\n\t\t\tvar body io.ReadCloser\n\t\t\tvar ferr error\n\t\t\tif cfg.CFDomain != \"\" {\n\t\t\t\tbody, _, ferr = b2Backend.Get(ctx, cfg.Bucket, key)\n\t\t\t} else {\n\t\t\t\tbody, _, ferr = b2Backend.GetDirect(ctx, cfg.Bucket, key)\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t\tif ferr != nil {\n\t\t\t\treturn nil, ferr\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t\tdefer body.Close()\n\t\t\treturn io.ReadAll(body)\n\t\t}\n\t\tloadStart := time.Now()\n\t\tif loadErr := manifest.Load(context.Background(), manifestIdx, cfg.ManifestPrefix, cfg.WriterID, lister, fetcher); loadErr != nil {\n\t\t\tlogger.WithFields(map[string]interface{}{\n\t\t\t\t\"error\": loadErr.Error(),\n\t\t\t}).Warn(\"manifest startup load failed — continuing with empty manifest index\")\n\t\t\tmanifestIdx = manifest.New() // reset to empty on error\n\t\t} else {\n\t\t\tlogger.WithFields(map[string]interface{}{\n\t\t\t\t\"entries\": manifest writer (async delta persistence to B2).\n\t// Uploads go direct to B2 (free ingress); no Cloudflare path needed here.\n\tvar manifestWriter *manifest.Writer\n\tvar manifestCompactor *manifest.Compactor\n\tif manifestIdx != nil {\n\t\tuploader := func(ctx context.Context, key string, data []byte) error {\n\t\t\treturn b2Backend.Put(ctx, cfg.Bucket, key, bytes.NewReader(data), backend.\n\t\tlisterForCompactor := func(ctx context.Context, prefix, token string) ([]string, string, error) {\n\t\t\tresult, lerr := b2Backend.ListRaw(ctx, cfg.Bucket, prefix, \"\", token, 1000)\n\t\t\tif lerr != nil {\n\t\t\t\treturn nil, \"\", lerr\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t\tkeys := make([]string, len(result.Objects))\n\t\t\tfor i, obj := range result.Objects {\n\t\t\t\tkeys[i] = obj.Key\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t\treturn keys, result.NextToken, nil\n\t\t}\n\t\tdeleter := func(ctx context.Context, keys []string) error {\n\t\t\treturn b2Backend.DeleteObjects(ctx, cfg.Bucket, keys)\n\t\t}\n\t\tcompactionInterval := time.Duration(cfg.ManifestCompactionInterval) * time.Second\n\t\tmanifestCompactor = manifest.NewCompactor(\n\t\t\tmanifestIdx,\n\t\t\tcfg.ManifestPrefix,\n\t\t\tcfg.WriterID,\n\t\t\tuploader,\n\t\t\tlisterForCompactor,\n\t\t\tdeleter,\n\t\t\tcompactionInterval,\n\t\t\tcfg.ManifestCompactionThreshold,\n\t\t)\n\n\t\t// Wire writer → compactor: after each delta flush, notify compactor.\n\t\tmanifestWriter.SetOnFlush(manifestCompactor.NotifyDelta)\n\n\t\tmanifestWriter.Start(context.Background())\n\t\tmanifestCompactor.Start(context.Background())\n\t\tlogger.Info(\"manifest writer and compactor started\")\n\t}\n\n\treturn &Server{\n\t\tconfig:         cfg,\n\t\tbackend:        b2Backend,\n\t\tcache:          cache,\n\t\tfooterCache:    footerCache,\n\t\tlistCache:      listCache,\n\t\tkeyManager:     keyMgr,\n\t\tcanary:         canaryMonitor,\n\t\tcanaryDisabled: cfg.CanaryDisabled,\n\t\tprovenance:     provenanceMgr,\n\t\tpresigner:      presigner,\n\t\tb2keys:         b2keysClient,\n\t\tdashboard:      dash,\n\t\tmanifest:          manifestIdx,\n\t\tmanifestWriter:    manifestWriter,\n\t\tmanifestCompactor: manifestCompactor,\n\t\tmetrics:        metrics.DefaultMetrics,\n\t\trequestTracker: metrics.DefaultRequestTracker,\n\t\tlogger:         logger,\n\t}, nil\n}\n\n// manifestRecorder implements handlers.ManifestRecorder. It updates the\n// in-memory index synchronously (so subsequent HeadObject calls see the new\n// state immediately) and enqueues the op for async B2 delta persistence.\ntype manifestRecorder struct {\n\tidx    *manifest.Index\n\twriter *manifest.Writer\n}\n\nfunc (m *manifestRecorder) RecordPut(bucket, key string, size int64, sha256Hex string, iv, wrappedDEK []byte, blockSize int, contentType, etag string) {\n\tentry := &manifest.Entry{\n\t\tPlaintextSize:   size,\n\t\tPlaintextSHA256: sha256Hex,\n\t\tIV:              iv,\n\t\tWrappedDEK:      wrappedDEK,\n\t\tBlockSize:       blockSize,\n\t\tContentType:     contentType,\n\t\tETag:            etag,\n\t\tLastModified:    time.Now().UTC(),\n\t}\n\tm.idx.Put(bucket, key, entry)\n\tm.writer.EnqueuePut(bucket, key, entry)\n}\n\nfunc (m *manifestRecorder) RecordDelete(bucket, key string) {\n\tm.idx.Delete(bucket, key)\n\tm.writer.EnqueueDelete(bucket, key)\n}\n\nfunc (m *manifestRecorder) Lookup(bucket, key string) (*handlers.ManifestEntry, bool) {\n\tentry, ok := m.idx.Get(bucket, key)\n\tif !ok {\n\t\treturn nil, false\n\t}\n\treturn &handlers.ManifestEntry{\n\t\tPlaintextSize: entry.PlaintextSize,\n\t\tContentType:   entry.ContentType,\n\t\tETag:          entry.ETag,\n\t\tLastModified:  entry.LastModified,\n\t\tIV:            entry.IV,\n\t\tWrappedDEK:    entry.WrappedDEK,\n\t\tBlockSize:     entry.BlockSize,\n\t}, true\n}\n\n// StopManifestWriter flushes any pending manifest ops and stops the async writer.\nfunc (s *Server) StopManifestWriter() {\n\tif s.manifestWriter != nil {\n\t\ts.manifestWriter.Stop()\n\t\ts.logger.Info(\"manifest writer stopped\")\n\t}\n}\n\n// StopManifestCompactor stops the background compaction goroutine.\nfunc (s *Server) StopManifestCompactor() {\n\tif s.manifestCompactor != nil {\n\t\ts.manifestCompactor.Stop()\n\t\ts.logger.Info(\"manifest compactor stopped\")\n\t}\n}\n\n// StartCanary starts the canary monitor.\n// It should be called after the server is created.\n// When ARMOR_CANARY_DISABLED=true, the monitor is not started and /readyz\n// always returns 200 regardless of B2 reachability.\nfunc (s *Server) StartCanary(ctx context.Context) {\n\tif s.canary == nil || s.canaryStarted {\n\t\treturn\n\t}\n\tif s.canaryDisabled {\n\t\ts.logger.Info(\"Canary monitor disabled (ARMOR_CANARY_DISABLED=true)\")\n\t\treturn\n\t}\n\ts.canaryStarted = true\n\ts.canary.Start(ctx)\n\ts.logger.Info(\"Canary monitor started\")\n}\n\n// StopCanary stops the canary monitor.\nfunc (s *Server) StopCanary() {\n\tif s.canary != nil && s.canaryStarted {\n\t\ts.canary.Stop()\n\t\ts.logger.Info(\"Canary monitor stopped\")\n\t}\n}\n\n// Handler returns the main S3 API handler.\nfunc (s *Server) Handler() http.Handler {\n\tmux := http.NewServeMux()\n\n\t// Health endpoints\n\tmux.HandleFunc(\"/healthz\", s.healthz)\n\tmux.HandleFunc(\"/readyz\", s.readyz)\n\n\t// Share endpoint for pre-signed URLs (public, no auth required)\n\tmux.HandleFunc(\"/share/\", s.handleShare)\n\n\t// S3 operations\n\th := handlers.New(s.config, s.backend, s.cache, s.footerCache, s.keyManager, s.listCache)\n\n\t// Wire up provenance if available\n\tif s.provenance != nil {\n\t\th.WithProvenance(s.provenance)\n\t}\n\n\t// Wire up manifest recorder if enabled\n\tif s.manifest != nil && s.manifestWriter != nil {\n\t\th.WithManifest(&manifestRecorder{idx: s.manifest, writer: s.manifestWriter})\n\t}\n\n\t// Bucket operations\n\tmux.HandleFunc(\"/\", s.wrapHandler(h.HandleRoot))\n\n\treturn mux\n}\n\n// AdminHandler returns the admin API handler.\nfunc (s *Server) AdminHandler() http.Handler {\n\tmux := http.NewServeMux()\n\n\tmux.HandleFunc(\"/healthz\", s.healthz)\n\tmux.HandleFunc(\"/admin/key/verify\", s.verifyKey)\n\tmux.HandleFunc(\"/admin/key/rotate\", s.rotateKey)\n\tmux.HandleFunc(\"/admin/key/export\", s.exportKey)\n\tmux.HandleFunc(\"/armor/canary\", s.canaryHandler)\n\tmux.HandleFunc(\"/armor/audit\", s.audit)\n\tmux.HandleFunc(\"/admin/presign\", s.handlePresign)\n\tmux.HandleFunc(\"/admin/b2/keys\", s.handleB2Keys)           // GET=List, POST=Create\n\tmux.HandleFunc(\"/admin/b2/keys/\", s.handleB2KeyDelete)     // DELETE=Delete by ID\n\tmux.HandleFunc(\"/metrics\", s.metrics.Handler())\n\n\t// Dashboard routes (authenticated via DashboardUser/Pass or DashboardToken)\n\tif s.dashboard != nil {\n\t\tmux.HandleFunc(\"/dashboard\", s.dashboard.HandlerWithAuth())\n\t\tmux.HandleFunc(\"/dashboard/\", s.dashboard.HandlerWithAuth()) // For prefix navigation\n\t\tmux.HandleFunc(\"/dashboard/object\", s.dashboard.ObjectDetailHandlerWithAuth())\n\t\tmux.HandleFunc(\"/dashboard/metrics\", s.dashboard.MetricsHandlerWithAuth())\n\t\tmux.HandleFunc(\"/dashboard/encryption-stats\", s.dashboard.EncryptionStatsHandlerWithAuth())\n\n\t\t// Key rotation proxy handler (authenticated)\n\t\tadminClient := &http.Client{\n\t\t\tTimeout: 30 * time.Minute, // Key rotation can take a long time\n\t\t}\n\t\tadminURL := \"http://\" + s.config.AdminListen + \"/admin/key/rotate\"\n\t\tmux.HandleFunc(\"/dashboard/admin/key/rotate\", s.dashboard.KeyRotateHandlerWithAuth(adminClient, adminURL))\n\t\tmux.HandleFunc(\"/dashboard/admin/key/status\", s.dashboard.KeyRotateStatusHandlerWithAuth())\n\t}\n\n\treturn mux\n}\n\n// healthz returns the health status.\n// This is the liveness probe — it only checks that the process is alive.\n// Backend connectivity is checked by /readyz (the readiness probe).\nfunc (s *Server) healthz(w http.ResponseWriter, r *http.Request) {\n\tw.WriteHeader(http.StatusOK)\n\tw.Write([]byte(\"OK\"))\n}\n\n// readyz returns the readiness status.\n// When the canary monitor is running and not disabled, its in-memory health\n// state is the sole signal — no backend call is made. When the canary is\n// disabled (ARMOR_CANARY_DISABLED=true), /readyz always returns 200 and the\n// liveness probe (/healthz) is the sole health guard. When the canary is not\n// configured, the manifest writer's last flush is used as the health signal.\nfunc (s *Server) readyz(w http.ResponseWriter, r *http.Request) {\n\t// When canary is explicitly disabled, skip all backend checks.\n\tif s.canaryDisabled {\n\t\tw.WriteHeader(http.StatusOK)\n\t\tw.Write([]byte(\"Ready\"))\n\t\treturn\n\t}\n\n\t// Canary monitor is authoritative when running.\n\tif s.canary != nil && s.canaryStarted {\n\t\tif !s.canary.IsHealthy() {\n\t\t\tw.WriteHeader(http.StatusServiceUnavailable)\n\t\t\tw.Write([]byte(\"Not ready - canary check failed\"))\n\t\t\treturn\n\t\t}\n\t\tw.WriteHeader(http.StatusOK)\n\t\tw.Write([]byte(\"Ready\"))\n\t\treturn\n\t}\n\n\t// Fallback: manifest writer's last successful delta flush.\n\t// A flush within the last 60 seconds indicates the service is healthy.\n\tconst flushThreshold = 60 * time.Second\n\tif s.manifestWriter != nil {\n\t\tlastFlush := s.manifestWriter.LastFlush()\n\t\tif !lastFlush.IsZero() && time.Since(lastFlush) < flushThreshold {\n\t\t\tw.WriteHeader(http.StatusOK)\n\t\t\tw.Write([]byte(\"Ready\"))\n\t\t\treturn\n\t\t}\n\t\t// No recent flush — report unhealthy\n\t\tw.WriteHeader(http.StatusServiceUnavailable)\n\t\tif lastFlush.IsZero() {\n\t\t\tw.Write([]byte(\"Not ready - manifest writer has never flushed\"))\n\t\t} else {\n\t\t\tfmt.Fprintf(w, \"Not ready - manifest writer last flush %v ago (threshold %v)\", time.Since(lastFlush).Round(time.Second), flushThreshold)\n\t\t}\n\t\treturn\n\t}\n\n\t// Neither canary nor manifest writer available — report unhealthy.\n\tw.WriteHeader(http.StatusServiceUnavailable)\n\tw.Write([]byte(\"Not ready - no health signal available\"))\n}\n\n// verifyKey verifies the MEK is correct.\nfunc (s *Server) verifyKey(w http.ResponseWriter, r *http.Request) {\n\tif r.Method != http.MethodGet {\n\t\thttp.Error(w, \"Method not allowed\", http.StatusMethodNotAllowed)\n\t\treturn\n\t}\n\n\tif s.canary == nil {\n\t\tw.WriteHeader(http.StatusOK)\n\t\tw.Write([]byte(`{\"status\":\"unknown\",\"error\":\"canary monitor not configured\"}`))\n\t\treturn\n\t}\n\n\tstatus := s.canary.GetStatus()\n\tif status.DecryptVerified && status.HMACVerified {\n\t\tw.WriteHeader(http.StatusOK)\n\t\tw.Write([]byte(`{\"status\":\"verified\",\"message\":\"MEK is correct\"}`))\n\t\treturn\n\t}\n\n\tw.WriteHeader(http.StatusServiceUnavailable)\n\tw.Write([]byte(`{\"status\":\"unverified\",\"error\":\"canary check failed - MEK may be incorrect\"}`))\n}\n\n// rotateKey rotates the MEK.\nfunc (s *Server) rotateKey(w http.ResponseWriter, r *http.Request) {\n\tif r.Method != http.MethodPost {\n\t\thttp.Error(w, \"Method not allowed\", http.StatusMethodNotAllowed)\n\t\treturn\n\t}\n\n\t// Read the new MEK from the request body\n\tbody, err := io.ReadAll(r.Body)\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\thttp.Error(w, fmt.Sprintf(\"Failed to read request body: %v\", err), http.StatusBadRequest)\n\t\treturn\n\t}\n\tdefer r.Body.Close()\n\n\t// The new MEK should be a 32-byte hex-encoded string (64 hex chars)\n\t// or raw 32 bytes\n\tvar newMEK []byte\n\tif len(body) == 64 {\n\t\t// Hex-encoded\n\t\tnewMEK, err = hex.DecodeString(string(body))\n\t\tif err != nil {\n\t\t\thttp.Error(w, \"Invalid hex-encoded MEK\", http.StatusBadRequest)\n\t\t\treturn\n\t\t}\n\t} else if len(body) == 32 {\n\t\t// Raw bytes\n\t\tnewMEK = body\n\t} else {\n\t\thttp.Error(w, fmt.Sprintf(\"Invalid MEK length: expected 32 bytes or 64 hex chars, got %d\", len(body)), http.StatusBadRequest)\n\t\treturn\n\t}\n\n\t// Create key rotator with the default key. Pass the manifest index so\n\t// rotateObject can skip per-object HeadObject calls when the entry is cached.\n\tdefaultKey := s.keyManager.DefaultKey()\n\trotator := NewKeyRotator(s.backend, s.config.Bucket, defaultKey.MEK, newMEK, s.manifest)\n\n\t// Perform rotation\n\tresult, err := rotator.Rotate(r.Context())\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\tw.WriteHeader(http.StatusInternalServerError)\n\t\tjson.NewEncoder(w).Encode(map[string]interface{}{\n\t\t\t\"status\":  \"failed\",\n\t\t\t\"error\":   err.Error(),\n\t\t\t\"result\":  result,\n\t\t})\n\t\treturn\n\t}\n\n\t// Update the server's MEK on success\n\tif result.Status == \"completed\" {\n\t\tif err := s.keyManager.UpdateDefaultKey(newMEK); err != nil {\n\t\t\ts.logger.WithFields(map[string]interface{}{\n\t\t\t\t\"error\": err.Error(),\n\t\t\t}).Error(\"failed to update key manager after rotation\")\n\t\t}\n\t\t// Clear the metadata cache since DEKs are now wrapped with new MEK\n\t\ts.cache.Clear()\n\t}\n\n\tw.Header().Set(\"Content-Type\", \"application/json\")\n\tw.WriteHeader(http.StatusOK)\n\tjson.NewEncoder(w).Encode(result)\n}\n\n// exportKey exports the current MEK.\nfunc (s *Server) exportKey(w http.ResponseWriter, r *http.Request) {\n\tif r.Method != http.MethodGet {\n\t\thttp.Error(w, \"Method not allowed\", http.StatusMethodNotAllowed)\n\t\treturn\n\t}\n\n\tif r.URL.Query().Get(\"confirm\") != \"yes\" {\n\t\thttp.Error(w, \"Must include ?confirm=yes to export key\", http.StatusBadRequest)\n\t\treturn\n\t}\n\n\t// Export the default MEK as hex-encoded string\n\tdefaultKey := s.keyManager.DefaultKey()\n\tw.Header().Set(\"Content-Type\", \"application/json\")\n\tw.WriteHeader(http.StatusOK)\n\tjson.NewEncoder(w).Encode(map[string]string{\n\t\t\"mek\":   hex.EncodeToString(defaultKey.MEK),\n\t\t\"format\": \"hex\",\n\t\t\"warning\": \"This key provides access to all encrypted data. Store securely.\",\n\t})\n}\n\n// canaryHandler returns the canary status.\nfunc (s *Server) canaryHandler(w http.ResponseWriter, r *http.Request) {\n\tif r.Method != http.MethodGet {\n\t\thttp.Error(w, \"Method not allowed\", http.StatusMethodNotAllowed)\n\t\treturn\n\t}\n\n\tif s.canary == nil {\n\t\tw.WriteHeader(http.StatusOK)\n\t\tw.Write([]byte(`{\"status\":\"unknown\",\"error\":\"canary monitor not configured\"}`))\n\t\treturn\n\t}\n\n\tstatus := s.canary.GetStatus()\n\tw.Header().Set(\"Content-Type\", \"application/json\")\n\tw.WriteHeader(http.StatusOK)\n\tjson.NewEncoder(w).Encode(status)\n}\n\n// audit returns the audit status.\nfunc (s *Server) audit(w http.ResponseWriter, r *http.Request) {\n\tif r.Method != http.MethodGet {\n\t\thttp.Error(w, \"Method not allowed\", http.StatusMethodNotAllowed)\n\t\treturn\n\t}\n\n\t// Create auditor and perform audit\n\tauditor := provenance.NewAuditor(s.backend, s.config.Bucket)\n\tresult, err := auditor.Audit(r.Context())\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\tw.WriteHeader(http.StatusInternalServerError)\n\t\tjson.NewEncoder(w).Encode(map[string]interface{}{\n\t\t\t\"status\": \"error\",\n\t\t\t\"error\":   err.Error(),\n\t\t})\n\t\treturn\n\t}\n\n\tw.Header().Set(\"Content-Type\", \"application/json\")\n\tw.WriteHeader(http.StatusOK)\n\tjson.NewEncoder(w).Encode(result)\n}\n\n// wrapHandler wraps a handler with common middleware.\nfunc (s *Server) wrapHandler(h http.HandlerFunc) http.HandlerFunc {\n\treturn func(w http.ResponseWriter, r *http.Request) {\n\t\tstart := time.Now()\n\n\t\t// Track in-flight request\n\t\ts.requestTracker.Start()\n\t\tdefer s.requestTracker.End()\n\n\t\t// Log request\n\t\ts.logger.WithFields(map[string]interface{}{\n\t\t\t\"method\": r.Method,\n\t\t\t\"path\":   r.URL.Path,\n\t\t}).Debug(\"incoming request\")\n\n\t\t// Add CORS headers for browser clients\n\t\tw.Header().Set(\"Access-Control-Allow-Origin\", \"*\")\n\t\tw.Header().Set(\"Access-Control-Allow-Methods\", \"GET, PUT, DELETE, HEAD, POST, OPTIONS\")\n\t\tw.Header().Set(\"Access-Control-Allow-Headers\", \"Authorization, Content-Type, Range, Content-Length\")\n\n\t\t// Handle preflight\n\t\tif r.Method == http.MethodOptions {\n\t\t\tw.WriteHeader(http.StatusOK)\n\t\t\treturn\n\t\t}\n\n\t\t// Verify auth for non-public endpoints\n\t\tif !s.isPublicPath(r.URL.Path) {\n\t\t\tcred, err := s.verifyAuthAndGetCredential(r)\n\t\t\tif err != nil {\n\t\t\t\ts.writeError(w, \"AccessDenied\", \"Invalid credentials\", 403)\n\t\t\t\ts.metrics.IncRequestsTotal(\"auth\", 403)\n\t\t\t\treturn\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t// Check ACL for the request. For list operations the URL path has no\n\t\t\t// key component, so fall back to the ?prefix query param so that ACL\n\t\t\t// prefix restrictions are enforced correctly against the listed prefix.\n\t\t\tbucket, key := s.extractBucketAndKey(r)\n\t\t\tif key == \"\" {\n\t\t\t\tkey = r.URL.Query().Get(\"prefix\")\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t\tif err := CheckACL(cred, bucket, key); err != nil {\n\t\t\t\ts.writeError(w, \"AccessDenied\", \"Access Denied\", 403)\n\t\t\t\ts.metrics.IncRequestsTotal(\"acl\", 403)\n\t\t\t\treturn\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t}\n\n\t\t// Decode aws-chunked body when MinIO streaming signature is used.\n\t\t// The seed signature in the Authorization header already authenticated the\n\t\t// request; we only need to strip the chunk framing to recover the payload.\n\t\tif r.Header.Get(\"X-Amz-Content-Sha256\") == \"STREAMING-AWS4-HMAC-SHA256-PAYLOAD\" {\n\t\t\tif decoded := r.Header.Get(\"X-Amz-Decoded-Content-Length\"); decoded != \"\" {\n\t\t\t\tif n, err := strconv.ParseInt(decoded, 10, 64); err == nil {\n\t\t\t\t\tr.ContentLength = n\n\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t\tr.Body = newAWSChunkedReader(r.Body)\n\t\t}\n\n\t\t// Use a response writer wrapper to capture status code\n\t\trw := &responseWriter{ResponseWriter: w, statusCode: http.StatusOK}\n\n\t\th(rw, r)\n\n\t\t// Record metrics\n\t\tduration := time.Since(start)\n\t\ts.metrics.IncRequestsTotal(r.Method, rw.statusCode)\n\t\ts.metrics.RecordRequestDuration(r.Method, duration)\n\n\t\t// Log completed request\n\t\tfields := map[string]interface{}{\n\t\t\t\"method\":      r.Method,\n\t\t\t\"path\":        r.URL.Path,\n\t\t\t\"status\":      rw.statusCode,\n\t\t\t\"duration_ms\": duration.Milliseconds(),\n\t\t}\n\t\tif rng := r.Header.Get(\"Range\"); rng != \"\" {\n\t\t\tfields[\"range\"] = rng\n\t\t}\n\t\ts.logger.WithFields(fields).Info(\"request completed\")\n\t}\n}\n\n// responseWriter wraps http.ResponseWriter to capture the status code.\ntype responseWriter struct {\n\thttp.ResponseWriter\n\tstatusCode int\n}\n\n// WriteHeader captures the status code.\nfunc (rw *responseWriter) WriteHeader(code int) {\n\trw.statusCode = code\n\trw.ResponseWriter.WriteHeader(code)\n}\n\n// isPublicPath checks if a path is public (no auth required).\nfunc (s *Server) isPublicPath(path string) bool {\n\treturn path == \"/healthz\" || path == \"/readyz\"\n}\n\n// verifyAuthAndGetCredential validates AWS SigV4 authentication and returns the credential.\nfunc (s *Server) verifyAuthAndGetCredential(r *http.Request) (*config.Credential, error) {\n\t// Create auth with all credentials\n\tauth := NewSigV4AuthWithCredentials(s.config.Credentials, s.config.B2Region)\n\n\t// Check for query-based auth (presigned URLs)\n\tif r.URL.Query().Get(\"X-Amz-Credential\") != \"\" {\n\t\treturn auth.VerifyQueryAuth(r)\n\t}\n\n\t// Check for header-based auth\n\tauthHeader := r.Header.Get(\"Authorization\")\n\tif authHeader == \"\" {\n\t\treturn nil, ErrMissingAuthHeader\n\t}\n\n\t// Pass nil body — buildCanonicalRequest uses x-amz-content-sha256 header\n\t// when present (which covers all AWS SDK/CLI requests), falling back to\n\t// sha256(body) for requests without that header.\n\treturn auth.VerifyRequest(r, nil)\n}\n\n// extractBucketAndKey extracts bucket and key from the request URL.\nfunc (s *Server) extractBucketAndKey(r *http.Request) (bucket, key string) {\n\tpath := r.URL.Path\n\t// Remove leading slash\n\tpath = strings.TrimPrefix(path, \"/\")\n\n\t// Check for virtual-hosted-style (bucket in host)\n\t// For path-style: /bucket/key\n\tparts := strings.SplitN(path, \"/\", 2)\n\tif len(parts) >= 1 {\n\t\tbucket = parts[0]\n\t}\n\tif len(parts) >= 2 {\n\t\tkey = parts[1]\n\t\t// URL decode the key (DuckDB httpfs encodes special chars like = as %3D)\n\t\tif decoded, err := url.PathUnescape(key); err == nil {\n\t\t\tkey = decoded\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\t// Use configured bucket if empty\n\tif bucket == \"\" {\n\t\tbucket = s.config.Bucket\n\t}\n\n\treturn bucket, key\n}\n\n// writeError writes an S3 error response.\nfunc (s *Server) writeError(w http.ResponseWriter, code, message string, statusCode int) {\n\tw.Header().Set(\"Content-Type\", \"application/xml\")\n\tw.WriteHeader(statusCode)\n\tvar codeBuf, msgBuf bytes.Buffer\n\txml.EscapeText(&codeBuf, []byte(code))\n\txml.EscapeText(&msgBuf, []byte(message))\n\tfmt.Fprintf(w, `<?xml version=\"1.0\" encoding=\"UTF-8\"?>`+\"\\n<Error>\\n  <Code>%s</Code>\\n  <Message>%s</Message>\\n</Error>\",\n\t\tcodeBuf.String(), msgBuf.String())\n}\n\n// GenerateDEK generates a new DEK (exposed for handlers).\nfunc (s *Server) GenerateDEK() ([]byte, error) {\n\treturn crypto.GenerateDEK()\n}\n\n// GenerateIV generates a new IV (exposed for handlers).\nfunc (s *Server) GenerateIV() ([]byte, error) {\n\treturn crypto.GenerateIV()\n}\n\n// WaitForInFlightRequests waits for all in-flight requests to complete.\nfunc (s *Server) WaitForInFlightRequests() {\n\ts.requestTracker.Wait()\n}\n\n// InFlightRequestCount returns the current number of in-flight requests.\nfunc (s *Server) InFlightRequestCount() int64 {\n\treturn s.requestTracker.Count()\n}\n\n// handlePresign generates a pre-signed URL for sharing encrypted files.\n// POST /admin/presign\n// Body: {\"bucket\": \"my-bucket\", \"key\": \"path/to/file.parquet\", \"expires_in\": \"1h\", \"content_disposition\": \"attachment; filename=\\\"file.parquet\\\"\"}\nfunc (s *Server) handlePresign(w http.ResponseWriter, r *http.Request) {\n\tif r.Method != http.MethodPost {\n\t\thttp.Error(w, \"Method not allowed\", http.StatusMethodNotAllowed)\n\t\treturn\n\t}\n\n\t// Verify auth\n\tcred, err := s.verifyAuthAndGetCredential(r)\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\ts.writeError(w, \"AccessDenied\", \"Invalid credentials\", 403)\n\t\treturn\n\t}\n\n\t// Parse request body\n\tvar req struct {\n\t\tBucket             string `json:\"bucket\"`\n\t\tKey                string `json:\"key\"`\n\t\tExpiresIn          string `json:\"expires_in\"`\n\t\tContentDisposition string `json:\"content_disposition\"`\n\t\tRange              string `json:\"range\"`\n\t}\n\n\tif err := json.NewDecoder(r.Body).Decode(&req); err != nil {\n\t\thttp.Error(w, fmt.Sprintf(\"Invalid request body: %v\", err), http.StatusBadRequest)\n\t\treturn\n\t}\n\n\t// Use configured bucket if not specified\n\tbucket := req.Bucket\n\tif bucket == \"\" {\n\t\tbucket = s.config.Bucket\n\t}\n\n\t// Validate required fields\n\tif req.Key == \"\" {\n\t\thttp.Error(w, \"key is required\", http.StatusBadRequest)\n\t\treturn\n\t}\n\n\t// Check ACL for the request\n\tif err := CheckACL(cred, bucket, req.Key); err != nil {\n\t\ts.writeError(w, \"AccessDenied\", \"Access Denied\", 403)\n\t\treturn\n\t}\n\n\t// Parse expiration (default 1 hour)\n\texpiration := presign.DefaultExpiration\n\tif req.ExpiresIn != \"\" {\n\t\texpiration, err = presign.ParseExpiration(req.ExpiresIn)\n\t\tif err != nil {\n\t\t\thttp.Error(w, fmt.Sprintf(\"Invalid expires_in: %v\", err), http.StatusBadRequest)\n\t\t\treturn\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\t// Build options\n\tvar opts []presign.Option\n\tif req.ContentDisposition != \"\" {\n\t\topts = append(opts, presign.WithContentDisposition(req.ContentDisposition))\n\t}\n\tif req.Range != \"\" {\n\t\topts = append(opts, presign.WithRange(req.Range))\n\t}\n\n\t// Generate pre-signed URL\n\tshareURL, err := s.presigner.GenerateURL(bucket, req.Key, expiration, opts...)\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\thttp.Error(w, fmt.Sprintf(\"Failed to generate URL: %v\", err), http.StatusInternalServerError)\n\t\treturn\n\t}\n\n\t// Return response\n\tw.Header().Set(\"Content-Type\", \"application/json\")\n\tjson.NewEncoder(w).Encode(map[string]interface{}{\n\t\t\"url\":       shareURL,\n\t\t\"expires_in\": presign.FormatExpiration(expiration),\n\t\t\"expires_at\": time.Now().Add(expiration).UTC().Format(time.RFC3339),\n\t})\n}\n\n// handleShare serves decrypted content from a pre-signed URL token.\n// GET /share/<token>\nfunc (s *Server) handleShare(w http.ResponseWriter, r *http.Request) {\n\tif r.Method != http.MethodGet {\n\t\thttp.Error(w, \"Method not allowed\", http.StatusMethodNotAllowed)\n\t\treturn\n\t}\n\n\t// Extract token from path\n\ttokenStr := presign.ParseTokenFromPath(r.URL.Path)\n\tif tokenStr == \"\" {\n\t\thttp.Error(w, \"Missing token\", http.StatusBadRequest)\n\t\treturn\n\t}\n\n\t// Verify token\n\ttoken, err := s.presigner.VerifyToken(tokenStr)\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\tif errors.Is(err, presign.ErrExpiredToken) {\n\t\t\thttp.Error(w, \"Link expired\", http.StatusGone)\n\t\t\treturn\n\t\t}\n\t\tif errors.Is(err, presign.ErrInvalidSignature) {\n\t\t\thttp.Error(w, \"Invalid link\", http.StatusForbidden)\n\t\t\treturn\n\t\t}\n\t\thttp.Error(w, \"Invalid token\", http.StatusBadRequest)\n\t\treturn\n\t}\n\n\t// Get object metadata\n\tctx := r.Context()\n\tinfo, err := s.backend.Head(ctx, token.Bucket, token.Key)\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\thttp.Error(w, fmt.Sprintf(\"Object not found: %v\", err), http.StatusNotFound)\n\t\treturn\n\t}\n\n\t// Check if object is ARMOR-encrypted\n\tif !info.IsARMOREncrypted {\n\t\t// Serve non-ARMOR objects directly (passthrough)\n\t\tbody, _, err := s.backend.Get(ctx, token.Bucket, token.Key)\n\t\tif err != nil {\n\t\t\thttp.Error(w, fmt.Sprintf(\"Failed to get object: %v\", err), http.StatusInternalServerError)\n\t\t\treturn\n\t\t}\n\t\tdefer body.Close()\n\n\t\tw.Header().Set(\"Content-Length\", fmt.Sprintf(\"%d\", info.Size))\n\t\tw.Header().Set(\"Content-Type\", info.ContentType)\n\t\tif token.ContentDisposition != \"\" {\n\t\t\tw.Header().Set(\"Content-Disposition\", token.ContentDisposition)\n\t\t}\n\t\tw.WriteHeader(http.StatusOK)\n\t\tio.Copy(w, body)\n\t\treturn\n\t}\n\n\t// Parse ARMOR metadata\n\tarmorMeta, ok := backend.ParseARMORMetadata(info.Metadata)\n\tif !ok {\n\t\thttp.Error(w, \"Failed to parse object metadata\", http.StatusInternalServerError)\n\t\treturn\n\t}\n\n\t// Get the MEK for this object\n\tmek, err := s.keyManager.GetMEKByID(armorMeta.KeyID)\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\thttp.Error(w, \"Failed to get decryption key\", http.StatusInternalServerError)\n\t\treturn\n\t}\n\n\t// Unwrap DEK\n\tdek, err := crypto.UnwrapDEK(mek, armorMeta.WrappedDEK)\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\thttp.Error(w, \"Failed to unwrap DEK\", http.StatusInternalServerError)\n\t\treturn\n\t}\n\n\t// Create decryptor\n\tdecryptor, err := crypto.NewDecryptor(dek, armorMeta.IV, armorMeta.BlockSize)\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\thttp.Error(w, \"Failed to create decryptor\", http.StatusInternalServerError)\n\t\treturn\n\t}\n\n\t// Set response headers\n\tw.Header().Set(\"Content-Length\", fmt.Sprintf(\"%d\", armorMeta.PlaintextSize))\n\tw.Header().Set(\"Content-Type\", armorMeta.ContentType)\n\tw.Header().Set(\"Accept-Ranges\", \"bytes\")\n\tif token.ContentDisposition != \"\" {\n\t\tw.Header().Set(\"Content-Disposition\", token.ContentDisposition)\n\t}\n\n\t// Handle range request if specified in token or header\n\trangeHeader := token.Range\n\tif rangeHeader == \"\" {\n\t\trangeHeader = r.Header.Get(\"Range\")\n\t}\n\n\tif rangeHeader != \"\" {\n\t\ts.handleShareRangeRequest(w, r, token, decryptor, armorMeta, rangeHeader)\n\t\treturn\n\t}\n\n\t// Full object download\n\ts.handleShareFullObject(w, r, token, decryptor, armorMeta)\n}\n\n// handleShareFullObject handles full object downloads for share endpoint.\nfunc (s *Server) handleShareFullObject(w http.ResponseWriter, r *http.Request, token *presign.Token, decryptor *crypto.Decryptor, armorMeta *backend.ARMORMetadata) {\n\tctx := r.Context()\n\n\tblockSize := armorMeta.BlockSize\n\tblockCount := int(crypto.ComputeBlockCount(armorMeta.PlaintextSize, blockSize))\n\tplaintextSize := armorMeta.PlaintextSize\n\n\t// Calculate offsets\n\thmacTableOffset := crypto.HeaderSize + plaintextSize\n\thmacTableSize := int64(blockCount) * crypto.HMACSize\n\n\t// 1. Prefetch HMAC table\n\thmacBody, err := s.backend.GetRange(ctx, token.Bucket, token.Key, hmacTableOffset, hmacTableSize)\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\thttp.Error(w, fmt.Sprintf(\"Failed to fetch HMAC table: %v\", err), http.StatusInternalServerError)\n\t\treturn\n\t}\n\thmacTable, err := io.ReadAll(hmacBody)\n\thmacBody.Close()\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\thttp.Error(w, fmt.Sprintf(\"Failed to read HMAC table: %v\", err), http.StatusInternalServerError)\n\t\treturn\n\t}\n\n\t// 2. Stream data from Cloudflare\n\tstreamSize := crypto.HeaderSize + plaintextSize\n\tdataBody, err := s.backend.GetRange(ctx, token.Bucket, token.Key, 0, streamSize)\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\thttp.Error(w, fmt.Sprintf(\"Failed to get object stream: %v\", err), http.StatusInternalServerError)\n\t\treturn\n\t}\n\tdefer dataBody.Close()\n\n\t// 3. Read and discard header\n\theaderBuf := make([]byte, crypto.HeaderSize)\n\tif _, err := io.ReadFull(dataBody, headerBuf); err != nil {\n\t\thttp.Error(w, fmt.Sprintf(\"Failed to read header: %v\", err), http.StatusInternalServerError)\n\t\treturn\n\t}\n\n\t// 4. Write status before streaming\n\tw.WriteHeader(http.StatusOK)\n\n\t// 5. Stream decrypt\n\tencryptedBuf := make([]byte, blockSize)\n\tfor blockIndex := 0; blockIndex < blockCount; blockIndex++ {\n\t\tremaining := plaintextSize - int64(blockIndex)*int64(blockSize)\n\t\tactualBlockSize := int(min64(int64(blockSize), remaining))\n\n\t\tencryptedBuf = encryptedBuf[:actualBlockSize]\n\t\tn, err := io.ReadFull(dataBody, encryptedBuf)\n\t\tif err != nil && err != io.EOF && err != io.ErrUnexpectedEOF {\n\t\t\treturn\n\t\t}\n\t\tif n == 0 {\n\t\t\tbreak\n\t\t}\n\t\tencryptedBuf = encryptedBuf[:n]\n\n\t\t// Verify HMAC\n\t\thmacOffset := blockIndex * crypto.HMACSize\n\t\tif hmacOffset+crypto.HMACSize > len(hmacTable) {\n\t\t\treturn\n\t\t}\n\t\texpectedHMAC := hmacTable[hmacOffset : hmacOffset+crypto.HMACSize]\n\n\t\tmac := hmac.New(sha256.New, decryptor.HMACKey())\n\t\tindexBytes := make([]byte, 4)\n\t\tbinary.BigEndian.PutUint32(indexBytes, uint32(blockIndex))\n\t\tmac.Write(indexBytes)\n\t\tmac.Write(encryptedBuf)\n\t\tcomputed := mac.Sum(nil)\n\n\t\tif !hmac.Equal(computed, expectedHMAC) {\n\t\t\treturn\n\t\t}\n\n\t\t// encryptedBuf)\n\n\t\t// Write to client\n\t\tw.Write(decrypted)\n\t}\n}\n\n// handleShareRangeRequest handles range requests for share endpoint.\nfunc (s *Server) handleShareRangeRequest(w http.ResponseWriter, r *http.Request, token *presign.Token, decryptor *crypto.Decryptor, armorMeta *backend.ARMORMetadata, rangeHeader string) {\n\tctx := r.Context()\n\tplaintextSize := armorMeta.PlaintextSize\n\n\t// Parse range header\n\tstart, end, err := parseRangeHeader(rangeHeader, plaintextSize)\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\thttp.Error(w, \"Invalid range\", header\")\n\t}\n}\n\n// Test authentication middleware with Bearer token\nfunc TestAuthMiddlewareBearerToken(t *testing.T) {\n\tauth := NewAuthMiddleware(\"\", \"\", \"my-secret-token\")\n\n\t// Valid token\n\treq := httptest.NewRequest(http.MethodGet, \"/dashboard\", nil)\n\treq.Header.Set(\"Authorization\", \"Bearer my-secret-token\")\n\trec := httptest.NewRecorder()\n\n\tif !auth.Authenticate(rec, req) {\n\t\tt.Error(\"Expected authentication to succeed with valid token\")\n\t}\n\t// On success, Authenticate returns true and doesn't write to response\n\tif rec.Code != 0 && rec.Code != http.StatusOK {\n\t\tt.Errorf(\"Expected no error status on success, got %d\", rec.Code)\n\t}\n\n\t// Invalid token\n\treq = httptest.NewRequest(http.MethodGet, \"/dashboard\", nil)\n\treq.Header.Set(\"Authorization\", \"Bearer wrong-token\")\n\trec = httptest.NewRecorder()\n\n\tif auth.Authenticate(rec, req) {\n\t\tt.Error(\"Expected authentication to fail with invalid token\")\n\t}\n\tif rec.Code != http.StatusUnauthorized {\n\t\tt.Errorf(\"Expected status 401 on invalid token, got %d\", rec.Code)\n\t}\n}\n\n// Test authentication middleware with no auth configured\nfunc TestAuthMiddlewareNoAuth(t *testing.T) {\n\tauth := NewAuthMiddleware(\"\", \"\", \"\")\n\n\treq := httptest.NewRequest(http.MethodGet, \"/dashboard\", nil)\n\trec := httptest.NewRecorder()\n\n\t// Should allow all when no auth configured\n\tif !auth.Authenticate(rec, req) {\n\t\tt.Error(\"Expected authentication to succeed when no auth configured\")\n\t}\n}\n\n//
